## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: nonlinear oscillator dynamics
**Analysis**: This task involves modeling the acceleration (dv/dt) of a nonlinear harmonic oscillator as a function of position, velocity, and time. The acceleration in such systems typically includes restoring forces (functions of x), damping terms (functions of v), and possibly driving forces (functions of t).

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Linear harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x (simple restoring force proportional to displacement)
- Damped harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (restoring force plus linear damping)
- Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 (cubic nonlinear restoring force)
- Duffing with damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (cubic nonlinearity plus damping)
- Driven Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * cos(c4 * t) (forced cubic oscillator)
- Van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * (1 - x**2) * v (nonlinear damping dependent on position)
- Quintic nonlinearity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5 (higher-order restoring force)
- Quadratic nonlinearity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 (asymmetric restoring force)
- Nonlinear damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (cubic velocity damping)
- Driven linear oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * sin(c3 * t) (sinusoidally driven damped oscillator)
- Pendulum-like: dv_dt = c0 * sin(c1 * x) (sinusoidal restoring force approximating pendulum)
- Rayleigh oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (Rayleigh-type nonlinear damping)
- Combined nonlinear: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * (1 - x**2) * v + c3 * cos(c4 * t) (full Duffing-Van der Pol with driving)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope ŌåÆ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects ŌåÆ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay ŌåÆ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior ŌåÆ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects ŌåÆ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Odd-power restoring forces (x, x**3, x**5) ŌåÆ symmetric potential well / hardening or softening spring nonlinearity
- Position-dependent damping coefficient (1 - x**2)*v ŌåÆ self-sustained oscillation (limit cycle) as in Van der Pol
- Cubic position term with opposite sign to linear term ŌåÆ double-well potential / bistability in Duffing systems
- Periodic driving terms cos(c*t) or sin(c*t) ŌåÆ forced oscillation, resonance, and chaos in nonlinear oscillators
- Odd-power velocity terms (v**3) ŌåÆ nonlinear energy dissipation / amplitude-dependent damping
- Sinusoidal function of position sin(c*x) ŌåÆ large-amplitude pendulum dynamics beyond small-angle approximation
- Mixed position-velocity products (x*v, x**2*v) ŌåÆ nonlinear coupling between restoring and dissipative forces
- Absence of explicit time dependence ŌåÆ autonomous system / conservative or self-excited oscillator

**Candidate 1:** `(c0*x + c1 + (c2*v + c3)*(c4*x + c5*v + c6*x*sin(c7 + t) + x**3))/(c2*v + c3)`

**Candidate 2:** `c0*sin(t) + c1*v*(c2 + x)**c3`
